- **Why parent-count is sound (empirically verified):** v0.43.0 (correct merge-commit release) = 2 parents, DL-171 derivable in-range; v0.32.0 (the incident) = 1 parent, per-PR refs collapsed into the release-line `(#123)`. A merge-commit tip is provably ref-complete; a non-merge tip is the only state where a squash could have silently dropped refs. CI checks out `fetch-depth:0`, so parents are real (a shallow graft would read parentless → the helper returns non-merge = fail-loud-safe).
- **`skipped` is NOT in the fail guard (adversarial-review fix):** a squash release whose sibling cards were already promoted (a partial/earlier run) has `moved==0, skipped>0` and MUST still fail; the legit idempotent merge-commit re-run is exempted by the tip check, not by `skipped`. An earlier draft gated on `skipped==0` and would have let that exact re-run-after-incident shape slip through.
- **Prevention not available (re-verified):** GitHub can't enforce a per-PR merge method — repo-wide allow-flags are all-or-nothing, disabling squash repo-wide breaks the feature-PR workflow, and rulesets expose no required-merge-method rule. So DETECTION stays the guard, paired with the merge-commit-for-release-PRs convention (VERSIONING.md).
- **Shared script — converges the 3-way drift:** `bin/promote-released-cards` is meant byte-identical across agent-board-toolkit (canonical), agent-webhook-bridge, and kanban-board, but had drifted (bridge carried DL-165's blanket exit-2; toolkit/kanban had no 0-promoted guard + the toolkit-only FR-2 `PROMOTE_PAGE_CAP`). This lands the cause-aware guard in the canonical and re-syncs all three to identical (toolkit PR + kanban DL-175). Paired shift-left: `release-pr-body` now surfaces cardless shipped DLs in the release PR body (pre-merge), so the post-merge promote rarely meets a cardless surprise.
- **Consequences:** `bin/promote-released-cards` (`merge_commit_tip` helper + cause-aware exit). Validated on the live board (canon #9): non-merge+cardless → exit 2; non-merge+already-released → exit 2 (the hole fix); merge+cardless → exit 0; merge+already-released idempotent re-run → exit 0; `--dls` cardless → exit 0. Bash — no PHPUnit harness; real-surface dry-runs are authoritative. No app code, no migration, no receiver change.

## DL-173 — `bridge:check` warns on a dl_number card with `source=null` (or an unmapped source) on a ref-mode writeback board (#3399)

- **Date:** 2026-06-29
- **Context:** in `ref` correlation mode the writeback is repo-qualified — `correlateDl(board, DL-N, repo)` → `findCardsByRef(board, 'dl', 'DL-N', source=<owner/repo>)` (DL-167). The kanban derives a card's by-ref `source` ONLY from a `pr_url` payload (`github.com/<owner>/<repo>/pull/<N>`). A DL card stamped with `dl_number` but **no `pr_url`** has `source=null`, is excluded by the repo-qualified lookup, and silently never self-moves — the dispatch ledger shows only `dropped: no reactions`, indistinguishable from a legitimate no-match. FR-4 (DL-171) made every *permanent* writeback failure loud; this `source=null` **correlation miss** was the one remaining invisible class. Reproduced by Sola (unification) + AIMLA (by-ref bisection).
- **Decision:** a new `bridge:check` warning (warn-never-fail, like DL-030/DL-162). When `correlation=ref`, for each mapped board (deduped) enumerate its `dl_number` cards and flag any whose derived `source` is null (no/again-non-GitHub `pr_url`) or matches no repo mapped to that board, naming card id + DL. New `KanbanClient::readBoardCards` (public diagnostic paged read, surfaces the `truncated` flag so an incomplete read doesn't give a false all-clear); `CheckCommand::checkWritebackSourceCoverage` + `derivedSource` (a FAITHFUL mirror of the kanban's `ExternalReferenceNormalizer::sourceFor()` — `payload.repo` with a `/`, else `pr_url`/`issue_url`/`html_url`, else `external_link` — kept in sync; the bridge re-derives because `tasks/search.json` doesn't return the kanban's computed external_references).
- **Adversarial-review fix:** a narrow first cut mirrored only `pr_url` → it would have FALSE-warned (`source=null … NEVER self-move`) cards the kanban sources via `repo`/`issue_url`/`html_url`/`external_link` — a confidently-wrong diagnostic, the exact failure mode this check exists to avoid. Widened to the full `sourceFor` mirror; added a payload.repo-sourced silent-path test.
- **Applies to single-repo boards too (corrects the FR's premise):** `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` passes the event repo to `correlateDl` UNCONDITIONALLY, so source-qualification is active on every ref-mode board, not just multi-repo ones — a `source=null` card is excluded even on a single mapped repo (verified: board 8 / card #3359). The check keys on `correlation=ref`, not repo count. `scan` mode omits source (immune) → no check.
- **Consequences:** `app/Console/Commands/Bridge/CheckCommand.php` (+ `checkWritebackSourceCoverage`/`sourceFromPrUrl`), `app/Bridge/Writeback/KanbanClient.php` (`readBoardCards`); 2 tests (source=null warns; mapped pr_url silent). Complements the tool-side root-cause fix (`kbcard --pr-url`, toolkit #3388) + the on-ramp docs. No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects; pint clean, phpstan L7 0, phpunit 66/66.

## DL-174 — Repo-qualified correlation only on SHARED boards (fixes the silent 1:1-board writeback no-op)

- **Date:** 2026-07-08
- **Context:** Board-8 card #3692, found during live merge-time verification of the kanban writeback (kanban PR #411 / DL-185): the `pull_request.closed` event classified to a no-op although the PR title carried the DL token and the card's `dl_number` matched. Root cause: `correlateDl`/`correlatePr` in `ref` mode pass the event's repo as the kanban `source` qualifier **unconditionally** (DL-167), and kanban's `source` filter is strict — a card whose derived refs carry `source=null` (every operator-stamped `dl_number` card with no `pr_url`/`repo` payload field) returns `{data:[]}`. Proven side-by-side: `by-ref?system=dl&ref=DL-185` → card 3411; the same query `+source=kanban-board` → `[]`. Effect: **no organic DL-correlated move has fired since DL-167 landed** on this install (dispatch ledger shows only dependabot-channel deliveries — that path creates its own `pr_url`-carrying, source-qualified cards). #3399/DL-173 had already named the failure mode and shipped a `bridge:check` warning + the tool-side `kbcard --pr-url` stamp; but a DL card is created *before* its PR exists, so the tool-side stamp cannot cover the `opened` correlation on a fresh card. Note: the v0.42 changelog's claim "single-repo board ⇒ no `source` key" never matched the code (the qualifier was unconditional from birth) — DL-173's "correlation passes the repo unconditionally" is the accurate statement.
- **Decision:** qualify only where ambiguity exists. `WritebackConfig::boardIsShared(boardId)` (two or more repo mappings targeting one `board_id`); the classifier (PR + push paths) and the dependabot handler (correlate + dedup re-correlate) pass the repo to `correlateDl`/`correlatePr` **only for shared boards**, else `null` → no `source` key. Shared-board installs (the multi-repo adopters DL-167 was built for, whose refs are `pr_url`-qualified) keep byte-identical strict behavior; 1:1 boards regain correlation for null-source cards with zero per-card stamping burden. The dependabot `cardsForRepo` pr_url attribution stays as the belt-and-suspenders foreign-card guard on all boards.
- **Diagnostic alignment:** the DL-173 `bridge:check` source-coverage warn now fires the `source=null … NEVER self-move` case only for **shared** boards (on a 1:1 board it would be a false alarm post-fix); the `source matches no mapped repo` warn stays on all boards (operator error either way).
- **Consequences:** `WritebackConfig` (+`boardIsShared`), `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` (both correlation sites), `KanbanDependabotCardHandler` (both correlation sites), `CheckCommand::checkWritebackSourceCoverage`, `docs/writeback.md` shared-board callout, tests (config + classifier ref-mode pair + check-command pair). No config or schema change; no migration.

## DL-175 — Secret-bearing kanban `api_base_url` requires https (loopback-only cleartext)

- **Date:** 2026-07-08
- **Context:** Board-8 card #3574 (audit 2026-07-06). `UrlValidator::httpUrl` accepted `http` OR `https`; the kanban `api_base_url` is where the writeback sends the bearer token on every call and where `bridge:provision` POSTs the freshly-generated webhook HMAC secret. An operator setting `BRIDGE_KANBAN_API_BASE_URL=http://…` shipped both in cleartext with no warning. Live installs use https — hardening, not an active exposure.
- **Decision:** new `UrlValidator::secureHttpUrl` — `httpUrl` + reject `http` unless the host is loopback (`127.0.0.1` / `localhost` / `::1`, the local-dev rig case with no wire exposure). Applied fail-closed at all three consumers: `WritebackClientFactory::make`, `bridge:provision` (before constructing the client), and `bridge:check` (error, fails the check). Deliberately NO env escape hatch: an internal-network hostname is exactly the case where "it's private anyway" quietly ships credentials in cleartext; a dev rig binds loopback. `receiver_base_url` and the github base keep plain `httpUrl` (not secret-bearing on our side; out of card scope). Operator approval per the receiver/secrets gate: 2026-07-08.
- **Consequences:** `UrlValidator`, `WritebackClientFactory`, `ProvisionCommand`, `CheckCommand`, `config/bridge.php` comment, `.env.example`, `tests/Unit/Support/UrlValidatorTest.php`. Existing https installs unaffected; an http-configured install now fails loud at the first token-bearing call instead of leaking.

## DL-176 — GitHub dedup key derives from the SIGNED body, not the unsigned `X-GitHub-Delivery` header

- **Date:** 2026-07-08
- **Context:** Board-8 card #3573 (audit 2026-07-06). The at-least-once dedup gate is `UNIQUE(delivery_id)`. Kanban derives it from the SIGNED body (replay-safe); GitHub took it from the `X-GitHub-Delivery` HEADER — outside the HMAC (signature covers body bytes only). An actor who captured one validly-signed delivery could resend it with a fresh header and get a full re-dispatch (re-staged inbox intents, re-fired channel pushes). Blast radius bounded (writeback is idempotent + no-regression-guarded) = duplicate notifications, not corruption.
- **Decision:** `GitHubAdapter` sets `delivery_id = sha256(raw body)` — 64 hex chars, exactly the column width; the header stays REQUIRED (envelope contract) but untrusted and unused. Chosen over a signed-timestamp freshness window (GitHub signs no timestamp; a body-derived key is deterministic and needs no clock). Consequence, deliberate: GitHub's operator "Redeliver" button now dedups too — the sanctioned reprocess path is `bridge:replay <id>` (which exists precisely for this). Distinct legitimate events never share a body (GitHub payloads carry ids/timestamps). Operator approval per the receiver/HMAC gate: 2026-07-08.
- **Consequences:** `GitHubAdapter` (+docblock), adapter tests (over-length-header test inverted to harmless), new e2e replay-dedup test, `CLAUDE_ARCHITECTURE.md` dedup-gate description. Kanban adapter unchanged (already body-derived). No migration (same column, new value shape for NEW github rows; old header-keyed rows remain valid history).

## DL-177 — `card#<task-id>` correlation channel (FR-7, framework v0.2.229)

- **Date:** 2026-07-08
- **Context:** Board-8 card #3652. The classifier correlated exclusively on `DL-NNN`, so cards without a decision-log number had NO automated move channel (every routine-fix card in the 2026-07-08 kanban batch was moved by hand). Filed upstream as FR-7; the framework shipped the token convention in v0.2.229 (spec co-owned; precedence rule confirmed by us and pinned).
- **Decision:** implement the bridge half exactly per spec: `\bcard#(\d+)\b` case-insensitive over `title + ' ' + head_ref` (PR path) and the branch ref (push path, `started` outcome) — the identical surface DL matching uses. Correlation is direct by native task-id: no source qualifier (globally-unique ids structurally sidestep the DL-174 null-source class), no classify-time kanban read (the durable handler already rejects a card not on the operator-mapped board — `card_not_on_mapped_board` — and applies the #2935 no-regression guard + `*_from_stages` allowlists). Trust model unchanged: the token only SELECTS the card; board + stage come from operator config. **Precedence:** `DL-NNN` wins when both tokens appear; the ignored `card#` is logged (degraded-states-loud) — our refinement, adopted into the framework contract verbatim.
- **Consequences:** `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` (`cardToken()` + PR/push fallbacks + precedence log), classifier tests (native-id selection with `Http::assertNothingSent`, case-insensitive branch match, precedence + log pin, push-path `started`), `docs/writeback.md` correlation-keys note. No config or schema change.

## DL-178 — Held auto-promote on `started` + pinned-card opt-out (framework contract PR #113)

- **Date:** 2026-07-09
- **Context:** Board-8 card #3744, toolkit card #3743. The operator wanted a Held/parked card to auto-move to In Progress when work genuinely begins (a branch is cut for it), by default, without re-introducing the accidental-movement hazard the original manual-only default protected against. Reconciled with the framework maintainer (sola-pm), who pinned the cross-mover contract in agent-board-framework PR #113: promote a Held card ONLY on a genuine branch **creation**; every ambiguous case is a no-op; a human can pin a card against auto-movement.
- **Decision:** the bridge already satisfies the genuine-creation requirement — `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` emits `started` only on `payload.created === true` (DL-160), so a re-push/force-push never re-fires it. No classifier change. Two things land: (a) the **Held-promote default** is delivered by carrying the board's Held stage id in the mapping's `started_from_stages` — the mechanism (DL-160's promote-from allowlist) is unchanged, only the operator's config default; (b) a **pinned-card opt-out** in the handler's `started` path — a non-empty `block_reason` OR a `no-automove` tag refuses the promotion regardless of stage, with a loud `warning` + the DL-171 `alert_channel` signal (`pinned_no_automove`). Scoped to `started` only (the work-start move); the four PR-lifecycle outcomes are untouched — pinning is about not un-parking a card, not about freezing its PR-driven lifecycle. Both `block_reason` and `tags` already ride the card GET, so no kanban-app change.
- **Consequences:** `KanbanMoveCardHandler::isPinned()` + the `started`-path guard; `KanbanMoveCardHandlerTest` (Held-promotes-when-configured control, block_reason refusal, no-automove-tag refusal); `docs/writeback.md` promote-from + opt-out notes. The toolkit `board-card-start` hook implements the same contract's local half (reflog creation-detection, card #3743). Operator action to activate the default: add the Held stage id to `started_from_stages` in the live `writeback.json` (a config edit, per the DL-160 deploy-ordering rule).

## DL-179 — Classifier resolves card-first tokens try-in-order-with-fallback: DL-unresolved falls through to a present `card#` (framework contract #112)

**Date:** 2026-07-09
**Context:** `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` committed to the `DL-NNN` path the moment a DL token was *present*, not when it *resolved*: `correlateDl()` returning `[]` was a **silent no-op** on both the `pull_request` and branch-create `push` paths, even when a `card#<id>` token was also in the title/branch. DL>card# precedence (DL-177) made DL win first, so adding `card#` to a DL-titled PR could not rescue a genuinely-decision-logged-but-unstamped card (the `payload.dl_number` stamp is manual and forgettable — the kanban #2179 class). Sibling dead-ends existed in the toolkit `board-card-start` hook (`if [ -z "$dl" ]`) and were already fixed in the reference reconciler (`kanban-prs-sync.py`, framework #111 item 4). The framework hardened the correlation contract in #112 and named kanban #3726 (toolkit) + bridge #3727 (this) as its implementers.

**Decision:** resolve card-first tokens on their **outcome**, in order, on both the PR and push paths:
1. `DL-NNN` **resolves** to card(s) → move them (the ratified, more-specific key). A co-present `card#` is logged `info` as ignored (a ref naming two cards is almost always an operator error; "the DL card moved but my card# didn't" must be diagnosable from the ledger).
2. `DL-NNN` **unresolved** → fall through to a present `card#` (the existing native-id move path).
3. (implicit) DL absent → `card#` path directly, unchanged.
4. A token was **present but nothing resolved** and there is no `card#` fallback → `Log::warning` a **high-value miss**; never a silent no-op.

**Board-scope guard — layer choice:** the `card#` fallback resolves by a *global* native id, but the move must stay scoped to the PR-repo's mapped board. Per #112's layer-flexibility clause, this classifier does **not** add its own board check — it stays classify-time-read-free — because `KanbanMoveCardHandler` already rejects a card not on the mapped board (`card_not_on_mapped_board`, DL-020) identically for DL and `card#` moves. The invariant (*no out-of-board card is moved, and the refusal is loud*) is satisfied in the durable handler.

**What did not change:** DL-resolved moves (single + bundled/DL-148), the dependabot `pr_number` path, the shared-board `source` qualifier (DL-167/174), the no-regression guard, and the `started` push trigger are all byte-identical for the resolving cases. The only behavior deltas are the two previously-dead branches: DL-unresolved-with-`card#` now **moves** (was silent), and DL-unresolved-without-`card#` now **warns** (was silent). Extracted a private `moveTargets()` to share the per-card target loop between the PR and push paths.

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Classifiers/GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier.php` (both paths restructured + `moveTargets` helper + class docblock), `tests/Feature/Classifiers/GitHubPrCardMoveClassifierTest.php` (3 new cases: PR fallthrough, PR high-value-miss warn, push fallthrough; existing precedence/no-match tests preserved), `docs/writeback.md` (precedence note rewritten to try-in-order-with-fallback). No migration, no config schema change, no receiver accept/reject change. phpunit 530/530, phpstan L7 0, pint clean.

## DL-180 — CI drift-gate for vendored agent-board-toolkit copies (pinned-version clone, not checked-in hash)

**Date:** 2026-07-09
**Context:** Toolkit card #3765, follow-up from #2615 (single-source bash toolkit). `bin/promote-released-cards` is vendored byte-identical from agent-board-toolkit, but byte-identity was enforced by discipline only (land in canonical → re-vendor); no CI failed a PR that edited the vendored copy in place. The script is release-critical — `release-promote-cards.yml` runs it with the writeback token — so silent drift fails quietly. The repo also never adopted the `.agent-board-toolkit-version` stamp that toolkit `INSTALL.md §6`/`UPGRADE.md §3` already prescribe. Design fork in the card (clone-at-pinned-tag vs checked-in expected-hash) dissolved on inspection: the toolkit's canonical `agent-board-toolkit-drift-check` already does content + version-skew checking against a toolkit checkout, the toolkit repo is public (unauthenticated clone, no secret plumbing), and "offline-stable" is moot since CI checks out from GitHub anyway. A checked-in hash would be a second mechanism for the same thing.

**Decision:** adopt the toolkit-prescribed model: check in `.agent-board-toolkit-version` (`0.10.0`) and add path-filtered `toolkit-drift.yml` that clones agent-board-toolkit at `v$(cat .agent-board-toolkit-version)` (`--depth 1 --branch`; a stamp naming no released tag fails the clone → fail-closed) and runs the toolkit's own `agent-board-toolkit-drift-check`. Path-filtered to `bin/**` + the stamp + the workflow itself — drift can only enter through those paths. Pinned checkout means a toolkit release does NOT break unrelated PRs here; the gate moves only when a re-vendor PR bumps the stamp (per UPGRADE.md §3, copy + stamp in the same PR).

**Consequences:** `.github/workflows/toolkit-drift.yml` (new), `.agent-board-toolkit-version` (new), CLAUDE.md rule 5 workflow enumeration. No app code, no behavior change; CI now fails on in-place edits to vendored toolkit tools — merge-blocking comes from the all-workflows-green dev-PR merge rule (CLAUDE.md rule 5), and the workflow is deliberately NOT a required status check (path-filtered checks never report on non-matching PRs and would block them; the laravel-tests.yml lesson). The gate guards divergence, not presence: a PR that deletes/renames the vendored file passes (accepted residual — visible in review, and `release-promote-cards.yml` fails loudly at next use). Under pinned checkout the drift-check's SKEW branch is structurally quiet in CI (toolkit@v<stamp> always has VERSION == stamp); the teeth are the content diff + fail-closed clone. Same decision mirrored in kanban-board as DL-195.

## DL-181 — Correction to DL-180: consume promote-released-cards as the SHA-pinned toolkit composite action; retire the vendored copy + drift-gate

**Date:** 2026-07-09

**Context:** DL-180 hardened the *vendored* `bin/promote-released-cards` with a CI drift-gate (`toolkit-drift.yml`), but the gate only detected divergence — it guarded a copy that shouldn't exist. Per the user-approved design decision (Option A on toolkit card #3768), the copy is eliminated: `agent-board-toolkit` v0.11.0 ships `promote-released-cards` as a **composite GitHub Action** (`promote/action.yml`), and this repo consumes it SHA-pinned. Drift becomes *impossible*, presence is guaranteed, and dependabot's `github-actions` ecosystem PRs the pin bumps — replacing the manual re-vendor ritual. Corrects the #2615 Decision #3 vendored-copy model for this repo's GitHub-Actions consumption.

**Decision:** in `release-promote-cards.yml`, replace the vendored-script run (+ the api_base injection step) with `uses: PupFuzz/agent-board-toolkit/promote@f48d8a692a45428dbbca1f419e17592e4d057845  # v0.11.0` (rule 8 SHA-pin format; the `# vX.Y.Z` comment is load-bearing for dependabot). The action absorbs the api_base injection into the checked-out `.release-pr.json`; the `KANBAN_API_BASE`/`KANBAN_EXPECTED_HOST` unset-preflight stays in the workflow. **Delete** `bin/promote-released-cards`, `.agent-board-toolkit-version`, and `.github/workflows/toolkit-drift.yml` (no vendored tool remains → the DL-180 gate retires). `fetch-depth: 0` + `fetch-tags` stay (the action derives the shipped-ref range from THIS repo's git history).

**Consequences:** `.github/workflows/release-promote-cards.yml` (rewritten promote step + header comment), `bin/promote-released-cards` (deleted), `.agent-board-toolkit-version` (deleted), `.github/workflows/toolkit-drift.yml` (deleted), `CLAUDE.md` rule 5 enumeration (Toolkit drift removed). No app code, no receiver/schema/config change. **DL-180's gate is superseded, not weakened** — the silent-drift failure mode it addressed is now structurally absent; the promote path's security guards live in the script (now fetched at the pinned SHA), byte-identical to what was vendored. Mirrored in kanban-board as DL-196. Toolkit card #3768.

## DL-182 — CI lint: card-id branches must carry a card#/DL correlation token in the PR title

**Date:** 2026-07-09
**Context:** The `card#<id>` / `DL-NNNN` PR-title token is the ONLY correlation key the GitHub-PR→card-move writeback has; a card-id branch (`<type>/<card-id>-slug`) whose PR title omits it merges fine but the tracking card silently never moves — empirically failed in wave-1 2026-07-08 (8 PRs, zero automated moves). No CI caught it. Reliability review of the card-movement chain after DL-180/DL-181 shipped; toolkit card #3770, board-12 home per the #3765 cross-repo-CI precedent. Mirrors kanban-board DL-197.

**Decision:** add `.github/workflows/pr-title-lint.yml` (`pull_request: [opened, edited, reopened]` — `edited` is load-bearing so a title fix re-runs; no checkout, reads event payload only; `permissions: contents: read`; `ubuntu-latest` runner). Pure-bash logic: skip (pass) `dependabot/**`, `release/**`, `sync/**`, `revert-*`, and any head branch not matching `^[a-z-]+/[0-9]+-`; for a card-id branch, extract the id and REQUIRE the title to contain a `card#<exact-id>` or `DL-[0-9]{1,4}` token bounded on BOTH sides (leading `(^|[^0-9A-Za-z])` + trailing `([^0-9]|$)`) so a coincidental substring can't satisfy it — `card#37700`, `discard#3770`, and `IDL-2` all fail — else `exit 1` naming the branch-derived id and both accepted forms. Title + branch are author-controlled and reach the script ONLY via the `env:` block, used quoted (`"$TITLE"`/`"$BRANCH"`) — never inline `${{ }}` in `run:` (Actions script-injection class). Mirrored in kanban-board as DL-197 (`[self-hosted, linux, x64]` runner).

**Consequences:** `.github/workflows/pr-title-lint.yml` (new), `CLAUDE.md` rule 5 workflow enumeration. No app code, no receiver/schema/config change. Converts the silent "card never moves" into a loud red check; merge-blocking comes from the all-workflows-green dev-PR merge rule (rule 5) — deliberately NOT a required status check (consistent with the drift-gate posture). **Documented limits (unsolvable here):** token-presence lint only — it cannot verify the id resolves to a real card or the RIGHT card; a cross-board work item (a board-12 card shipped via a kanban/bridge PR, e.g. #3765) passes the lint but still won't auto-move, because correlation is deliberately board-scoped 1:1 per repo (DL-174). The lint checks the convention, not end-to-end movement.

## DL-183 — `bridge:reconcile` — board-vs-GitHub drift reconciler (closes RC-B; eventually-consistent card movement)

**Date:** 2026-07-10
**Context:** The GitHub-PR→card-move writeback is purely event-driven, and GitHub delivers each webhook **exactly once with no auto-retry**. A bridge outage during a PR event (deploy, downtime) drops that card's move permanently — nothing re-drives it, and the only backstop was the manual `board-session-close`. This is RC-B, left open by the 2026-06-05 writeback-drift RCA (RC-A was closed by `release-promote-cards.yml`/DL-141). Reliability review of the card-movement chain after DL-180/181/182 shipped; bridge card #3769.

**Decision:** add `php artisan bridge:reconcile {--fix} {--repo=} {--max-moves=20}` (`app/Console/Commands/Bridge/ReconcileCommand.php`), default REPORT-ONLY (one line per drifted card + summary counts, exit 0; `--fix` applies the forward moves). It recomputes each tracked card's expected stage from **GitHub ground truth** via a new read-only `GitHubReadClient` (`GET /repos/{repo}/pulls/{n}`, token at `<secret_dir>/github/token` per the general per-provider convention — NOT the least-privilege kanban writeback token; the kanban-board repo is private so a `repo`-scoped read token is required). The REST-state→outcome mapping is the **same** as `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier`, sharing the extracted `PrOutcome::forMergedBase()` for the drift-prone merged→stage decision so the two paths can't diverge; the pinned-card predicate is extracted to a shared `PinGuard::isPinned()` (second real caller — canon #5). Only cards with a resolvable `(repo, PR)` are reconciled: a `pr_url` (yields both), or a `pr_number` on a 1:1 board (the mapping supplies the repo); a `dl_number`-only card is skipped-with-info (DL→PR needs a GitHub search, out of v1 scope), and a bare `pr_number` on a shared board is ambiguous→skipped.

**Guards (reused, not reinvented) + read-side loudness (DL-026 posture):** a STARTUP auth probe (`GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}` per mapped repo) fails LOUDLY + non-zero and skips that repo's cards, so an under-scoped/expired token can't silently 404 every card while the run exits 0 (both reviewers' top finding); never moves a card BACKWARD (DL-163 `boardStageOrder` — backward/unorderable drift is reported, never applied, and an *unorderable* drift exits non-zero rather than false-green); never moves a PINNED card (DL-178); treats `released_to_main` as TERMINAL keyed on the OUTCOME `merged_to_main` (not stage-id equality, so a board that maps `merged`==`merged_to_main` still advances merged-to-dev cards) — never out of it, never into it (release-promotion excluded; the promote workflow owns that stage); a TRUNCATED board read aborts that board loudly; `--max-moves` (default 20) aborts before applying ANY move when more are planned (mass movement = probably a bug); after the probe, a per-card 404 is a benign deleted-PR skip while a 401/403 (token revoked mid-run) exits non-zero. `bridge:check` gains a warn when writeback is configured but the github read token is absent/insecure.

**Consequences:** new `ReconcileCommand`, `GitHubReadClient`, `PrOutcome`, `PinGuard`; `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` + `KanbanMoveCardHandler` refactored to the shared primitives (pure extraction, behavior-identical, existing tests unchanged); `CheckCommand` github-token warn; docs (`docs/writeback.md` § Reconciliation, `CLAUDE_DEPLOYMENT.md` command table, `CLAUDE.md` quick-start). **No new cron** (the daemonless design accepts exactly one, `prune`) — operators schedule it from host cron or the session-close ritual; automating `--fix` is an operator choice (start report-only). No migration, no `.env` key, no receiver accept/reject change. **v1 scope limits (documented, deliberate):** DL-only cards and bare-pr_number-on-shared-board cards aren't reconciled (no resolvable repo,PR); the branch-create `started` outcome isn't reconciled (no PR to GET — self-heals on the next PR event); the `closed_unmerged` abandoned-PR *backward* regression is reported (accurately labelled) but not auto-applied — the reconciler declines all backward moves in v1, leaving that to the event path/redelivery or a human (a scope call flagged by the design reviewer; revisit if the abandoned-PR case proves common). DL→PR resolution and cron wiring are separate follow-ups if wanted.

## DL-184 — bridge:reconcile GitHub token: env + configurable path sources (reuse a centralized PAT natively)

**Date:** 2026-07-10
**Context:** `bridge:reconcile` (DL-183) reads GitHub PR state and read its token ONLY from the fixed path `<secret_dir>/github/token` via `GitHubReadClient::fromConfig()` — no env fallback, no configurable path. An install with a centralized credential store (e.g. the Agent Board Framework coord store at `~/.config/coord/`, whose GitHub PAT is exported as `GH_TOKEN` in `~/.bashrc` and file-backed at `~/.config/coord/github-pat`) could not reuse it natively; the operator had to symlink/copy the PAT into the bridge's own path per install. Card #3835 (consumer-driven). Note: a richer *store-native* named-key resolution (parse the coord `credentials.ini`, honor its inline→`_file`→env precedence, select via `[git-credential-map]`) is a **separate, deferred** item pending a framework-dev answer on the supported consumer contract — this DL is the framework-independent core only.

**Decision:** `GitHubReadClient` resolves the token from, in precedence order:
1. **`bridge.providers.github.token_path`** (env `BRIDGE_GITHUB_TOKEN_PATH`) — an explicit file path, `~`-expanded, perms-gated. **Authoritative when set**: a missing/blank/insecure file yields null-or-throw with **no** ambient fallback, so a wrong path fails loud (canon: never silently resolve a *different* credential than configured). Selects "which PAT" by pointing at that PAT's file.
2. **`<secret_dir>/github/token`** — the conventional per-provider path (unchanged back-compat default), when no override is set.
3. **`GH_TOKEN` env** — an ambient fallback used only when no override is set AND the conventional file is unplaced/blank. Present in an operator shell (`~/.bashrc`), absent in the webhook-spawned receiver (which never sources `~/.bashrc`), so the fallback self-scopes to the reconcile CLI with no receiver exposure. Trimmed; blank is ignored.

The DL-010 file-perms fail-closed gate is preserved for both file sources (a group/world-readable token file still throws); the env source has no file to gate (process-private by nature). `bridge:check` and the command's "no token" error now name the resolved source and mention all three.

**Consequences:** `config/bridge.php` (`providers.github.token_path`), `app/Bridge/Writeback/GitHubReadClient.php` (`tokenPath` override + `hasTokenPathOverride` + env fallback in `fromConfig`), `app/Console/Commands/Bridge/CheckCommand.php` + `ReconcileCommand.php` (source-aware messages), `docs/writeback.md` + `CLAUDE_DEPLOYMENT.md`, tests (`GitHubReadClientTest` + `ReconcileCommandTest`, made hermetic re ambient `GH_TOKEN`). No migration, no `.env` requirement (all optional), no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects — a CLI/operator-config surface only. Back-compat: an install with only the conventional file behaves identically. **Deferred to v2 (framework contract now confirmed):** store-native named-PAT resolution via the framework's **existing** `git-credential-coord get` helper (git wire-format on stdin/stdout, callable from PHP via `proc_open`) — do NOT parse `credentials.ini` (a fourth precedence copy would be drift; framework dev, coord v0.2.251, `docs/CREDENTIALS.md § Non-git consumers`). "Which PAT" resolves through `[git-credential-map]` (host/owner/repo → key, most-specific-first), NOT a hardcoded key name — key names vary by install role (`impl_readonly` on a PM install, only `coordination` on a solo install), and the map routes per-repo with least-privilege for free. The store-native leg inserts as the DEFAULT before the `GH_TOKEN` last leg with the guardrail: an ambient `GH_TOKEN` must never shadow a store-mapped token, and an empty resolver result is a real answer (fail loud on unmapped/`REPLACE_ME`, never fall through to a wrong-scoped token). Tracked as a follow-up card. Note per framework dev: reconcile makes the bridge's GitHub token a RUNTIME dependency (was provision-time only in the framework `docs/TOKENS.md #5`) — send the final token/selector shape post-release so that map stays honest.

## DL-185 — bridge:reconcile v2: store-native per-repo GitHub token (git-credential-coord + `[git-credential-map]`)

**Date:** 2026-07-10
**Context:** The DL-184 v2 follow-up (card #3841), now that the framework contract is confirmed (coord v0.2.252, `docs/CREDENTIALS.md § Non-git consumers (GitHub REST)`). DL-184 shipped the framework-independent core (token_path override + conventional file + `GH_TOKEN`); it can't reuse a *per-repo least-privilege* PAT from the coordination store. `bridge:reconcile` built ONE `GitHubReadClient` for every mapped repo, so a single token had to cover all of them.

**Decision:** Extract a **`GitHubTokenResolver`** (the single home of the precedence — canon #5; DL-184's `GitHubReadClient::fromConfig/tokenPath/hasTokenPathOverride` are removed, and `GitHubReadClient` is now token-agnostic) that resolves the token **per repo**:
1. **`token_path` override** (config) — authoritative; read only that file; blank/missing → fail loud; no store/env fallback. [DL-184]
2. **`<secret_dir>/github/token`** conventional file, when present. [DL-183/184]
3. **store-native** — `git-credential-coord get` (Laravel `Process` facade, shell-free argv, git wire-format on stdin), keyed on the store's `[git-credential-map]` (host/owner/repo, most-specific-first) → a per-repo least-privilege PAT. The default when no explicit token file is placed. [NEW]
4. **`GH_TOKEN`** env — the last leg. [DL-184]

`ReconcileCommand` now resolves + builds a `GitHubReadClient` **per repo** (memoized by canonical repo), in the existing startup probe loop; an unresolvable token skips only that repo's cards (loud, non-zero exit), consistent with the unreadable-repo isolation. `bridge:check` routes its "reconcile token available?" check through the **same resolver** (a non-throwing `TokenResolution`, so it stays warn-never-fail per DL-026 and can't drift from reconcile).

**Load-bearing decisions (from the fresh-adversarial design review):**
- **Missing helper ≠ a catchable start-exception.** On Symfony Process 8.x a missing binary returns **exit 127** (the failure is in the forked child), not a `ProcessStartFailedException` — so the helper is pre-resolved with `ExecutableFinder`/`is_executable` **before** spawning; not-found → leg-not-applicable → fall through to `GH_TOKEN` (this is what keeps a `GH_TOKEN`-only install, incl. prod, working). Relying on a start-exception would have broken prod.
- **Unreadable `*_file` must fail loud, not fall through.** The helper exits **0** with empty stdout on both the genuinely-unmapped case AND the unreadable-`*_file` case; the discriminator is **stderr** (non-empty only on the error path). So `exit0 + empty stdout + empty stderr` = unmapped → `GH_TOKEN`; `exit0 + empty stdout + non-empty stderr` = fail loud (honors the framework fail-loud-on-`*_file` contract + card guardrail 2). `exit≠0` and a resolved `REPLACE_ME` password also fail loud.
- **Raw repo key, not canonical.** `[git-credential-map]` is case-**sensitive** (`optionxform = str`); `ExternalReferenceNormalizer::canonicalizeSource()` lower-cases. The resolver is invoked with the **raw** `writeback.json` mapping key; only the client memoization is keyed by the canonical form.
- **Ordering (open question A): conventional file stays ABOVE store-native.** An explicit token file (override or `<secret_dir>/github/token`) short-circuits the store; store-native is the default only when no explicit file is placed (the common case, incl. prod). Documented footgun: placing a global token file while also mapping the repo in the store means the file wins (per-repo scoping disabled) — use `token_path`/the file, or the store map, not both.
- **`credential_helper` config knob** (`bridge.providers.github.credential_helper`, default `git-credential-coord`): PATH-resolved bare name, or an absolute path used as-is; empty disables the store leg. Dual purpose (nonstandard PATH + explicit opt-out + test seam).

**Guardrails honored (framework contract):** `GH_TOKEN` (4) is consulted only *after* the store (3) returns nothing → can never shadow a store-mapped token; `REPLACE_ME`/helper-crash/unreadable-`*_file` fail loud → never a silent fall-through to a wrong-scoped token. The bridge must guard `REPLACE_ME` itself: the installed helper has **no** `REPLACE_ME` guard (it emits `password=REPLACE_ME`), contradicting the doc's "REPLACE_ME yields no password= line" — a framework doc/helper discrepancy to relay.

**Consequences:** new `app/Bridge/Writeback/GitHubTokenResolver.php` + `TokenResolution.php`; `GitHubReadClient` stripped to construct/getPull/probeRepo; `ReconcileCommand` per-repo clients; `CheckCommand` routed through the resolver; `config/bridge.php` (`providers.github.credential_helper`, env `BRIDGE_GITHUB_CREDENTIAL_HELPER`); `docs/writeback.md` + `docs/config-schema.md`; tests (new `GitHubTokenResolverTest` exercising the store leg against a REAL stub helper — a subprocess, not `Process::fake`, so the exec/stderr/exit-code state machine is validated on the real surface; `GitHubReadClientTest` reduced to request-shape; `ReconcileCommandTest` + `BridgeCommandsTest` neutralize the store leg for determinism + a new per-repo store test). No migration, no `.env` requirement (all optional), no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects — a CLI/operator-config surface only. Back-compat: an install without a `[git-credential-map]` (or without the helper on PATH) resolves exactly as DL-184. **Runtime-env note (relay):** the helper is spawned inheriting the reconcile CLI env, so it needs `HOME`/`COORD_CREDENTIALS` to locate the store — fine for an interactive operator run; if reconcile is ever wired to a timer, those must be set in the unit. Still owed to framework dev post-release: the final DL-184/185 token/selector shape for `docs/TOKENS.md #5` (runtime-dependency correction) + the `REPLACE_ME` helper/doc discrepancy.

## DL-186 — bridge:reconcile token diagnosability: name the resolved leg + preflight validity probe + upgrade-shadow docs

**Date:** 2026-07-10
**Context:** Consumer-driven FR from TWO peer integrators (AIMLA PM + Sola PM), both hitting the same failure on their first `bridge:reconcile` run after upgrading to v0.48.0 (DL-184/185): every repo `401`s despite a correctly-populated `[git-credential-map]`. Root cause each time: a pre-existing conventional `<secret_dir>/github/token` (or `BRIDGE_GITHUB_TOKEN_PATH`) from the single-token era — dated before the upgrade, holding a **stale** token — silently short-circuits the store-native leg (leg 1/2 beat leg 3, by design). Nothing at runtime pointed at the offending file, and the `HTTP 401` error didn't say *which* of the 4 legs resolved the token, so it cost a full root-cause detour. This install (the reference solo install) is NOT exposed (no `<secret_dir>/github/token` file). **Not a correctness bug** — verified reconcile runs correctly (36 targeted + 569 full tests green; clean prod run); the precedence is sound and unchanged.

**Decision:** three diagnosability improvements, **no precedence behavior change** (the FR explicitly did not ask for one):
1. **Name the resolved leg on failure.** `GitHubTokenResolver` already computed `TokenResolution::source` (`token_path override (…)` / `token file (…)` / `store (git-credential-coord: repo)` / `GH_TOKEN`) but nothing surfaced it. `ReconcileCommand` now appends `(token from <source>)` to the per-repo auth-probe failure (both `RequestException` and connection branches) and prints a per-repo `readable (token from …)` line under `-v`. Never prints the token, only the leg.
2. **`bridge:check` validity probe.** The reconcile-token check was resolvability-only (a resolved-but-expired token passed preflight silently). It now, per mapped repo whose token *resolves*, probes `GET /repos/{repo}` with that token and **warns** (never fails — DL-026) on a non-2xx, naming the leg + the shadowing-file hint. A network/timeout (not a token-validity signal) stays silent. Adds ≤N GitHub calls to preflight (N = mapped repos), symmetric with the existing per-board visibility probes.
3. **Upgrade-shadow docs.** `docs/writeback.md` gains an UPGRADING callout (a pre-existing token file short-circuits the store map — remove it to adopt per-repo tokens) + a "Running reconcile unattended" worked example (cron/systemd `HOME`/`PATH`/`COORD_CREDENTIALS` for the helper, `--max-moves` circuit-breaker, operator-maintenance framing).

**Consequences:** `app/Console/Commands/Bridge/ReconcileCommand.php` (source in probe messages + `-v` line), `app/Console/Commands/Bridge/CheckCommand.php` (validity probe; `GitHubReadClient` + `RequestException` re-imported), `docs/writeback.md` + `docs/CHANGELOG.md`, tests (`ReconcileCommandTest` auth-probe-names-leg; `BridgeCommandsTest` resolved-token-invalid-warns + GH_TOKEN cleared in setUp for hermeticity now that the resolver can resolve via ambient GH_TOKEN). No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects, no precedence change. Card #3858.

## DL-187 — Writeback stamps a card# fallback card's dl_number/pr_number add-if-missing (release-promote correlation)

**Date:** 2026-07-10
**Context:** Cards the writeback moves via the `card#<id>` native-id fallback (DL-177/179) never carried `payload.dl_number`/`payload.pr_number`. `promote-released-cards` correlates released cards by exactly those payload fields (git-log-derived DL/PR sets), so a card# card with neither is invisible to release-promote — it strands in Shipped-to-Dev instead of Released (seen live on cards 3792/3841/3858 during the v0.30.1/v0.48.0 board reconcile; the pre-fix workaround is `kbcard --dl` at decision-time). The classifier already parses the correlation tokens from the PR title/branch; the handler never wrote them back. `KanbanClient::moveCard` is deliberately column-only. Grounded facts (verified): the kanban v3 API MERGES `task.payload` per-key ([[lesson-kanban-payload-patch-merges-per-key]] / kanban #2180), so the stamp is a delta PATCH — no read-merge-write; and moving a card and writing its payload are the SAME endpoint/permission/ability, so the least-privilege writeback token needs NO scope bump.

**Decision:** the writeback stamps a moved card's correlation refs, add-if-missing, as a step DISTINCT from the column-only move. Scoped tightly to eliminate corruption vectors a fresh-adversarial design review surfaced:
1. **Only the `card#` fallback path stamps** (both pull_request and branch-create push). A DL-resolved card already carries its `dl_number` (that is HOW it resolved), so stamping it delivers nothing for the gap — and threading `pr_number` onto it would poison a feature card from a release PR whose title names that card's DL. `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` threads `stamp_dl`/`stamp_pr` into the target payload on the card# path only.
2. **The DL is stamped only when EXACTLY ONE `DL-NNN` appears** in the title+branch (a bundled/release-shaped PR carrying 2+ DLs — or a single foreign, unresolved DL alongside a `card#` for a different card — stamps `pr_number` only). The sole-DL + `card#` shape is the intended "card created before its DL" case.
3. **`KanbanMoveCardHandler` stamps add-if-missing** (never overwrites an existing/human-set value; the already-read card payload is the authority — no extra read), formatting the DL as the canonical zero-padded `DL-%04d` every kbcard-written card uses. Placed AFTER the reject-guards (started/no-regression) and additionally in the already-in-stage self-heal branch — so a stale/redelivered/regressive event the guards no-op never stamps.
4. **Best-effort with the move's transient/permanent split:** a 4xx (e.g. the board lacks the `dl_number`/`pr_number` custom field) is permanent → log + no-op; a 5xx/timeout PROPAGATES → redelivery re-stamps (stamp is add-if-missing-idempotent, move is idempotent), closing the window where a swallowed transient failure would strand the card unstamped forever.

The stamp's `task.updated` webhook is echo-dropped for the writeback identity (and is not a move trigger regardless), so no re-classify loop. Backstop (a `promote-released-cards` WARN on a released DL with no card) was ALREADY present (`MISSING`/`nmiss`), so no tooling change.

**Alternatives considered:** (a) stamp on every move incl. the DL-resolved path — REJECTED (delivers nothing there + poisons `pr_number` from release PRs; the design-review must-fix). (b) read-merge-write the full payload — REJECTED (unnecessary given per-key merge, and reintroduces a lost-update race — see [[lesson-kanban-payload-patch-merges-per-key]]). (c) always-swallow stamp failures — REJECTED (a swallowed transient 5xx strands the card, the exact failure this closes).

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Classifiers/GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier.php` (new `titleAndHead` primitive + `dlToken`/`cardToken` refactored onto it; new `stampRefs`; stamp threaded into both card# targets), `app/Bridge/Handlers/KanbanMoveCardHandler.php` (new `stampCorrelationRefs` + two call sites), `app/Bridge/Writeback/KanbanClient.php` (new `stampCorrelationRefs` write verb; `moveCard` stays column-only), `docs/writeback.md`, tests (12 new: 5 classifier + 7 handler). 583/583 phpunit, phpstan L7 0, pint clean; one fresh-adversarial design-review pass (5 findings, all folded in). No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects, no token scope bump. Card #3866.

## DL-188 — Unified config-driven `CoordinationClassifier` + typed `ClassifierConfig` (roundtable-#8 classifier unification)

**Date:** 2026-07-11
**Context:** Three peer projects (kanban-solo / sola / aimla) each ran a bridge classifier that was a near-duplicate fork: GitHub coordination-message routing (DL-022 addressing + DL-002 shared-identity re-attribution), plus per-project extras — sola's `impl-ci-wake` (push→release-landed + `workflow_run` CI wake), the kanban triage-wake (DL-168), sola's `registry_append` + board-sync `spawn_detached`. Every install forked the classifier PHP because config could only reach a classifier through the untyped `AgentConfig::$raw` blob — there was no typed parameterization surface. Roundtable #8 converged on ONE reference classifier + a thin per-project config, so no install forks the bridge; the packaging follow-on (coord plugin stops shipping a classifier template, pins a min-bridge-version) is sola's, post-merge.

**Decision:** a single non-final, config-driven `CoordinationClassifier` that `extends InboxOnlyClassifier` and runs a **config-gated event-family pipeline** keyed on `classifier.config.families` ({@see ClassifierConfig}), landed in two commits under this DL:
1. **Core (PR #252, `d6731fa`):** the `coord-message` family (the pre-#8 behavior + §1 `scope_author_map` primary attribution) and the `impl-ci-wake` family (push→`release_branch` = release-landed with `subjectId = head_sha`; `workflow_run` **fail-LOUD** CI gate — wake on ANY terminal conclusion NOT in `benign_conclusions` [`success`,`cancelled`,`skipped`,`neutral`], so a new/unknown GitHub conclusion surfaces instead of silently escaping oversight; name-matched provenance-success wakes). `ClassifierConfig` is the typed view (`scope_author_map`, `families`, generic `strings()`/`string()`/`section()` accessors) so a family adds knobs without another contract change. DEFAULT families `[coord-message]` ⇒ an install that doesn't opt in behaves EXACTLY as the pre-#8 reference (back-compat). Reattribution is enrichment, never a filter.
2. **kanban-triage fold (this PR):** `CoordinationClassifier` now `extends InboxOnlyClassifier` (was `implements Classifier`) so `parent::classify()` provides base inbox-staging for kanban `task.*`; the new **`kanban-triage` family** folds the DL-168 untriaged-check in as a family (human-filed + no `triaged`/`id:pr:*` tag + no `dl` ref, off the DL-164 `card` snapshot — no API call → `channel_push` to the triage owner). The standalone `KanbanTriageClassifier` becomes a **thin back-compat shim** (`extends CoordinationClassifier`, `defaultFamilies() → [kanban-triage]`) — single implementation of the untriaged check (canon #5), while `classifier.class: …\KanbanTriageClassifier` keeps working for v0.42.0 adopters. The github families self-guard `provider === 'github'` (the pre-#8 top-level provider guard is gone). Sola-specifics (`registry_append`, board-sync `spawn_detached`) stay OUT of the base — they live in sola's thin L2 subclass.

**Scope-agnostic:** never branches on `$ctx->scopeId` for routing (keys on addressing labels + `$agent->agentName`), so one instance serves a coord repo, the cross-project channel, an impl repo, and a kanban triage board unchanged.

**Alternatives considered:** (a) keep three forked classifiers — REJECTED (canon #5, divergent duplication of the same behavior). (b) `impl-ci-wake` CI gate as an allow-set of wake-conclusions — REJECTED by both sola + aimla: an allow-set fails SILENT on a conclusion it doesn't enumerate; the exclude-set (`benign_conclusions`) fails loud. (c) retire `KanbanTriageClassifier` entirely — REJECTED (breaks the `classifier.class` target v0.42.0 installs adopted, for no gain over a 5-line shim; canon #3). (d) gate kanban inbox-staging behind the `kanban-triage` family — REJECTED (inbox-staging is the InboxOnly base behavior; a coord-only install is never subscribed to kanban events, so unconditional `parent::classify()` is a no-op for it).

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Support/ClassifierConfig.php` (new, core), `app/Bridge/Classifiers/CoordinationClassifier.php` (new core + `extends InboxOnlyClassifier` / `kanban-triage` family / `defaultFamilies()` in this fold), `app/Bridge/Classifiers/KanbanTriageClassifier.php` (→ shim in this fold), `docs/config-schema.md` (classifier.config keys + family enumeration), `docs/customization.md`. Tests: `ClassifierConfigTest` + `CoordinationClassifierTest` (kanban-triage family cases added; the `wake_conclusions` sample-key nit renamed to a neutral `sample_list`); `KanbanTriageClassifierTest` unchanged and green — proving shim back-compat. 609/609 phpunit, phpstan L7 0, pint clean. No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects. Requires kanban **v0.22.0+** for the `card` snapshot (degrades to over-wake on older — SessionStart untriaged-snapshot is the durable backstop). Card #3930. Adoption (per install): bridge upgrade → retire the local `CoordinationClassifier` overlay → set `classifier.config` (families + `scope_author_map` + `release_branch`); a windowed pass for any install whose live pm-wake bridge is the substrate (aimla). Prod release/deploy stays operator-gated.

## DL-189 — `CoordinationClassifier` R1 config knobs: `impl_repos` wake gate + `drop_title_all_of` coord noise filter (roundtable-#8 R1)

**Date:** 2026-07-12
**Context:** Roundtable-#8 R1: fold the genuinely fleet-generic slice of sola-PM's coordinator classifier into the shared reference (config-gated), holding the sola-specific coordinator model for a sola-side simplification examination. Two independent line-by-line reviews (sola + aimla, against `CoordinationClassifier.php@v0.50.0`) converged the R1 scope to exactly two knobs + one doc fix; the proposed `provenance_wake_exclude_scopes` was dropped as unreachable (a coord `Protocol integrity` success already returns null — it doesn't match `provenance_patterns`, so there is no wake to suppress; canon #6), and the coord-half "pm-wake profile" reconciliation was deferred (both kanban-solo and aimla run plain `coord-message` with no gap — the stage-all / surgical-wake / no-self-wake deltas are sola-PM coordinator elaboration backstopped by the SessionStart GitHub state-query, not fleet gaps).

**Decision:** two optional, config-gated knobs on the existing families (defaults reproduce v0.50.0 byte-for-byte):
1. **`impl_repos`** (list<string>, `impl-ci-wake`): an early-return at the top of `implCiWakeFamily` — when non-empty, the family fires only when `lower($ctx->scopeId)` is in the list; empty/absent ⇒ every subscribed repo (back-compat). Lets a PM subscribed to both a coord repo and impl repos scope the CI/push wake to the impl subset so a coord-repo push/CI event doesn't self-wake. Gates BEFORE `pushSignal`/`workflowRunSignal`, so the push-landing predicate and fail-loud conclusion logic are unchanged.
2. **`drop_title_all_of`** (list<list<string>>, `coord-message`): drop a coordination subject whose **title** contains every (case-insensitive) substring of any one group — AND within a group, OR across groups — before the recipient gate, for bookkeeping-title noise (e.g. `[["Rule E back-merge sync","paper-trail anchor"]]`). Empty/absent ⇒ no subject dropped. New typed accessor `ClassifierConfig::stringGroups()` (fail-closed like the others).

Also a doc-sync fix (aimla's catch): the `implCiWakeFamily` comments said a non-wake impl event is "staged to inbox by the dispatcher" — inaccurate. The dispatcher inbox-stages classifier **intents** only (`DispatchService` L143-145); a null family + empty InboxOnly base ⇒ no intent ⇒ the event is **gate-dropped** (`markDropped('classifier emitted no reactions')`), never inbox-staged. Comments corrected to match.

**Alternatives considered:** (a) `provenance_wake_exclude_scopes` to suppress a redundant coord provenance success — REJECTED (unreachable state; a `Protocol integrity` success is already null, canon #6). (b) genericize sola-PM's stage-all/surgical-wake coordinator model into `coord-message` — DEFERRED, not adopted: a second real coordinator install (aimla) runs plain `coord-message` with no gap, so it's a sola-side simplification, not a fleet knob (same validity-gate discipline as the R2 board-sync/registry split). (c) merge `coord-message` + `impl-ci-wake` into one `pm-wake` family — REJECTED (breaks their standalone composable uses; "pm-wake" is a documented config profile of two families, not a merged class — D1).

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Support/ClassifierConfig.php` (+`stringGroups()`), `app/Bridge/Classifiers/CoordinationClassifier.php` (impl_repos gate + drop_title_all_of drop + `titleMatchesDropGroup()` + corrected L219/L237 comments + family docstring), `docs/config-schema.md` (two new `classifier.config` keys). Tests added to `CoordinationClassifierTest` (impl_repos in/out/case-insensitive/empty; drop_title_all_of all/partial/case-insensitive/absent) + `ClassifierConfigTest` (`stringGroups` parse + 3 fail-closed cases). No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects. Both knobs default-empty ⇒ v0.50.0 behavior. Card #3977. Fleet adoption via `classifier.config` on the eventual bridge release; sola adopts after its coord-half simplification examination resolves.

## DL-190 — `CoordinationClassifier` Phase-2: the shared best-of-both impl base — 4 config knobs folding `SolaImplClassifier`'s features (roundtable-#8 Phase-2)

**Date:** 2026-07-13
**Context:** roundtable #8 Phase-2 (three-way converged: kanban-solo landing owner, sola + aimla sign-off). The coord + PM side unified at v0.50.0/v0.51.0; Phase-2 folds the remaining impl-agent classifier features into the tracked `CoordinationClassifier` so no install forks the bridge on the impl side either. Inventories: **aimla is adopt-only** (impl agents run plain `[coord-message]`, PM-dispatched-brief model, nothing to fold); **`SolaImplClassifier` is the sole fold source**. Its delta over the v0.51.0 `impl-ci-wake` family (which already covers `release_landed` + fail-loud `ci_failed` + provenance-success `provenance_ok` + the `impl_repos` gate) resolved to: `release` event = **drop** (sola doesn't classify it); impl-repo coord comments = **per-install config** (subscribe `issues`/`issue_comment` on code repos + `coord-message`, same DL-022/032 lineage, not code); and two genuine model differences + two coord-message refinements, landed as config knobs.

**Decision:** four config-gated knobs on `CoordinationClassifier`, every default reproducing v0.51.0 byte-for-byte **except `wake_membership`** (a deliberate, 3-way-agreed wide→narrow default flip):
- **`impl_non_wake_disposition: drop (default) | inbox_stage`** — a non-wake terminal impl event (benign completed `workflow_run`; non-release push) either gate-drops (default, lean inbox) or builds a no-`channel_push` inbox `Intent` (`impl_push`/`impl_ci`) for a broad SessionStart history. A non-terminal `workflow_run` / branch-delete push is never staged. This is sola's INBOX-broad model vs the surgical-wake default.
- **`impl_wake_emit: channel_push (default) | none`** — a wake-worthy event stages its `Intent` either way; `none` suppresses the classifier's surgical `channel_push` so a channel whose `route_intents:true` owns waking isn't double-woken (sola's 3 impl channels are `route_intents:true`; her profile is `{inbox_stage, none}`). **[SUPERSEDED by DL-191 — retired: the suppression is now derived from `route_intents`, all families, no knob. Never released to prod.]**
- **`coord_extra_actions: {prefix:[actions]}`** — extends the fail-safe `subject()` `HANDLED` allow-list per prefix (sola opts `{pull_request:[synchronize]}` in). **Kept an allow-list extension, NOT sola's proposed deny-list** — a deny-list is fail-open (a new GitHub action auto-surfaces for everyone), canon #3.
- **`wake_membership: [to_me, to_all] (NEW default) | +from_me (opt-in)`** — config-drives the `coord-message` `$forMe` gate. **Deliberate wide→narrow default flip:** `from_me` grants membership for **all** activity on threads you opened (a `from:<me>` issue label). Because a comment's direction lives in its **body `TO:` line** — not as a `to:<me>` issue label (which freezes at thread-open) — and the body-`TO:` check only *narrows* within membership, dropping `from_me` shifts even a **directed** reply on your own thread from live-wake to SessionStart pickup, not just the bare-no-`TO:` case. Narrow is the safe unified standard (over-wake is the failure mode); `from_me` becomes the opt-in; the shifted own-thread replies are backstopped by the `from:<self>`/`protocol:invalid` SessionStart scan. The comment-`TO:` narrowing is unchanged (still narrows within membership, can't grant). aimla + kanban-solo both ran wide before, both accept the flip (brief-replies shift live-wake → SessionStart `from:<self>`/`protocol:invalid` boundary pickup).
- **`github_user_id`-never-on-wake-identity invariant** — codified as a docblock on the shared `makeImplIntent` + a regression test: the wake identity is the author agent by NAME (via `scope_author_map`), never the raw pusher github id, so the dispatcher's pre-classify echo gate can't drop an agent's own-repo landing. A wake-purposed agent config must not set `identity.github_user_id`.

Rec **(a)** for sola's one coord-repo nuance (a self-generated `Protocol integrity` success): keep `impl-ci-wake` code-repo-scoped via `impl_repos` so coord-repo `workflow_run` never enters the family — no 6th knob; the failure signal is backstopped by the `protocol:invalid` SessionStart scan.

**Alternatives considered:** (a) a 6th `drop_workflow_names` knob for the coord-repo Protocol-integrity noise — REJECTED (config-scoping via `impl_repos` already solves it; canon #6). (b) a deny-list for `coord_extra_actions` (sola's first proposal) — REJECTED (fail-open). (c) enum-validate `impl_non_wake_disposition`/`impl_wake_emit` and throw on an unknown value — NOT adopted, for consistency with every other `ClassifierConfig` knob (unrecognized → default); the valid values are documented and sola replay-verifies at adoption. (d) fold `release` event handling — REJECTED (sola doesn't classify it; `release_landed` + `provenance_ok` cover the need).

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Support/ClassifierConfig.php` (+`stringListMap()`), `app/Bridge/Classifiers/CoordinationClassifier.php` (the 4 knobs + shared `makeImplIntent()` extraction + `pushInboxSignal()`/`workflowRunInboxSignal()` + family docstring), `docs/config-schema.md` (4 new `classifier.config` keys). 14 tests added to `CoordinationClassifierTest` (wake_membership narrow/opt-in/default; coord_extra_actions surface/fail-safe; inbox_stage stage/skip/wake-preserved; wake_emit none; sola composite profile; the identity invariant). 636/636 phpunit, phpstan L7 0, pint clean. **No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects.** Defaults reproduce v0.51.0 EXCEPT `wake_membership` (the agreed flip — a CHANGELOG **Upgrading** note ships at release: restore wide via `wake_membership: [to_me, to_all, from_me]`). Card #3977. Fleet adoption via `classifier.config` on the eventual bridge release; sola adopts `{inbox_stage, none, coord_extra_actions, [to_me,to_all]}` + replay-verifies, aimla enables `impl-ci-wake` via its #249 window.

## DL-191 — channel-aware wake-emit: suppress a family's `channel_push` when `route_intents:true`; retire `impl_wake_emit` (roundtable-#8 Phase-2 replay fix)

**Date:** 2026-07-13
**Context:** sola's Phase-2 replay-verify (against the DL-190 dev head `97ac39e`) found a residual double-wake her `route_intents:true` profile hits and `impl_wake_emit:none` doesn't cover: the **`coord-message`** family hand-emits a `channel_push` (`debounceKey → subjectId`), and on a `route_intents:true` channel the dispatcher ALSO routes every staged intent as a `channel_push` (`debounceKey = channel_push:<subjectId>`, `DispatchService:169-178`). Different dedup keys ⇒ both survive ⇒ **two pushes per addressed coord message**. `impl_wake_emit:none` only covered the impl-ci family; `kanban-triage` has the identical latent double-wake (sola corroborated). aimla independently corroborated the hazard is real — all four aimla channels were pinned `route_intents:false` months ago with an in-config note ("route_intents=true would double-push every event"). So the intended contract already existed by convention: **a hand-emitting classifier ⟺ `route_intents:false`.** Three-way converged (kanban-solo reference owner; sola + aimla both endorsed this over their own two proposals). sola profile: code-repo `pull_request`/`issues`/`issue_comment` drop under the unified model (route through coord-message's recipient gate → no `to:`/`from:` labels on a code-repo object → dropped) — **accepted + CHANGELOG-documented (F-B)**, confirmed cost-free by both non-owner installs (aimla can't hit it by architecture; sola's only loss is non-self/dependabot code-repo activity, already on the kanban-card path). Landless branch-delete drop (F-C) folds into the same note. `from:<self>` narrow-flip drop (F-D) is the agreed DL-190 flip, SessionStart-backstopped — no action.

**Decision:** encode the invariant **structurally at the classifier** (where the emit decision is made and `route_intents` is already visible via `$ctx->agent->channel->routeIntents`) rather than per-family knob or dispatcher change. A single `wakePush(Intent, ClassifyContext)` helper emits the surgical `channel_push` **only when `route_intents` is false**; when the channel routes, the dispatcher's routed push (byte-identical `$intent->toArray()` payload) is the single wake. Applied uniformly to all three families (`coord-message`, `impl-ci-wake`, `kanban-triage`). **Retires `impl_wake_emit`** (DL-190) — subsumed: `route_intents:true` auto-suppresses; `route_intents:false` keeps the surgical hand-emit; no install ran `{route_intents:false, none}` (dead surface, confirmed by all three).

**Alternatives considered:** (a) `coord_wake_emit: channel_push|none` mirroring `impl_wake_emit` (sola's lean) — REJECTED: a **second** per-family patch of one invariant; a third family needs a third knob (canon #5). (b) dispatcher-level coalesce — route_intents skips emitting a `channel_push` for a subject a classifier already hand-emitted one for — REJECTED: rewrites the deliberate `channel_push:`-namespace whose blast radius aimla flagged as a silent-missed-wake risk (canon #6/#14 — don't touch shared dispatch semantics for a problem the classifier layer solves cleanly).

**Load-bearing safety (verified in code, not asserted):** (1) **payload parity** — both hand-emit sites and the routed push all carry `payload: $intent->toArray()`, so suppress-and-route loses no wake. (2) **narrow `wake_membership` gate preserved** — `coordMessageFamily` returns `null` (no intent) for a non-member **before** the emit decision, so the staged-intent set == the would-push set; `route_intents` routing every staged intent cannot widen the wake past the gate. (3) **kanban-triage** — the base `InboxOnly` new_card intent is staged regardless, so under `route_intents:true` it routes (single wake), no miss; the triage push's selectivity was already defeated by base-intent routing on such a channel (pre-existing, not introduced). (4) **`route_intents:false` installs (aimla, kanban-solo)** — the routing block never runs → hand-emit unchanged → **byte-identical**.

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Classifiers/CoordinationClassifier.php` (+`wakePush()`; the 3 family emit sites route through it; `impl_wake_emit` read removed), `docs/config-schema.md` (`impl_wake_emit` row removed; `route_intents` row notes `CoordinationClassifier` is safe on either setting). 6 tests added / 2 retired in `CoordinationClassifierTest` (coord-message route_intents true/false + narrow-gate-on-route_intents; impl-ci suppress; sola inbox_stage-on-route_intents; kanban-triage suppress). 640/640 phpunit, phpstan L7 0, pint clean. **No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects.** `route_intents:false` = byte-identical; the only behavior change is on `route_intents:true` (single wake, was double). sola re-replays (harness extended to model the dispatch-level route_intents merge; asserts exactly one `channel_push` per addressed coord message) as the empirical close before the operator-gated prod release; aimla adopts zero-change on the release window. Card #3977 (Phase-2 umbrella). Bundled with DL-190 in the eventual bridge prod release. Coordinated in PupFuzz/agent-roundtable#8.

## DL-192 — `comment_to`: a body `TO:<self>` line GRANTS coord-message wake membership (opt-in three-state), closing the cross-thread pull-in gap

**Date:** 2026-07-13
**Context:** The DL-022 recipient gate is **label-authoritative**: `wake_membership` selects which *issue-label* classes grant live-wake, and a comment's body `TO:` line can only **narrow** (`RecipientAddressing::addresses === false` → deny), never grant. That leaves one addressing shape unreachable by any label: a **cross-thread pull-in** — a comment that adds `TO: <self>` on a thread the agent neither opened nor was labelled on. The `to:<me>` label freezes at thread-open, so a later loop-in-via-comment cannot express itself as a label and silently fails to wake. This bites the **PM/coordinator seat** shape specifically (it opens briefs labelled `to:<impl>`, not `to:<self>`), and it cost a live 3-round miss on roundtable #8 (workaround: hand-add a `to:<pm>` label). No `wake_membership` value is faithful: `from_me` covers brief-replies on your *own* threads but not a pull-in onto someone else's. Three-way converged in PupFuzz/agent-roundtable#17 (kanban-solo reference owner + implementer; sola FR author; aimla confirmed the shared gap at source, hit it live on #8).

**Decision:** add an opt-in `wake_membership` **member** `comment_to` (one config axis — NOT a separate `coord-message` sub-key). With `comment_to` set, the comment body `TO:` line becomes a full three-state gate via the shipped `RecipientAddressing::addresses` (one call, no second parse): `=== true` (addressed to me / `all`) → **GRANTS** membership independent of thread labels; `=== false` (addressed elsewhere) → **denies** (the existing narrow); `=== null` (no `TO:` line) → falls back to label membership. Load-bearing: the **narrow stays unconditional** (runs with or without `comment_to`, so every install keeps it) and `comment_to` adds **only** the `=== true → grant` — so the default `[to_me, to_all]` is **byte-identical**. The full PM-seat wake config becomes `[to_me, to_all, from_me, comment_to]` (`from_me` = brief-replies on own threads; `comment_to` = cross-thread pull-ins).

**Alternatives considered:** (a) a separate `coord-message` sub-key (`comment_to: grant`) — REJECTED: a second config axis for what `wake_membership` (the "which classes grant a wake" knob) already models; keep one axis (consistency with `from_me`/`impl_repos`/`drop_title_all_of`). (b) gating the whole three-state on `comment_to` — REJECTED: would make the *narrow* opt-in, silently regressing every install that relies on a comment addressed-elsewhere denying membership; the narrow must stay unconditional. (c) re-vendoring the retired `SolaPmClassifier::coordIntentAddressesPm` per-install — REJECTED: that is the fork the roundtable-#8 unification removed; policy belongs in config, machinery in the shipped primitive.

**Load-bearing safety (verified in code + test):** (1) **default byte-identical** — with `comment_to` absent the new `=== true` branch is unreachable; only the pre-existing `=== false` narrow and the label-derived membership run (`test_comment_to_off_by_default_does_not_grant`). (2) **narrow unconditional** — a comment `TO: other` denies even with `comment_to` set AND a `to:me` label present (`test_comment_to_narrow_still_denies_a_comment_addressed_elsewhere`). (3) **null falls back to labels** (`test_comment_to_null_body_falls_back_to_labels`). (4) **echo-gate ordering probe** — the grant fires label-independent, so a PM's *self*-authored `TO:<self>` comment is dropped by the dispatcher's pre-classify own-author echo suppression (DL-007) before this gate runs; a PM addresses `to:<impl>`, not itself, so the case is off-path, but the ordering was confirmed by exercising, not assertion.

**Consequences:** `app/Bridge/Classifiers/CoordinationClassifier.php` (the `$forMe` comment gate becomes the three-state grant/narrow/fallback + class docblock), `docs/config-schema.md` (`comment_to` added to the `wake_membership` value list + the "body-`TO:` never grants" claim corrected to "grants only with `comment_to`", Rule X1). 4 tests added to `CoordinationClassifierTest` (grant / off-default / narrow-unconditional / null-fallback). No `ClassifierConfig` schema change — `wake_membership` values are not allow-list-validated, so `comment_to` needs no new accessor. **No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects.** Default byte-identical; `comment_to` is purely additive. sola adopts it in its Half-B PM-classifier config-only migration; aimla opts in on board-10/roundtable seats — both on the release pact. Card #4138. Coordinated in PupFuzz/agent-roundtable#17.

## DL-193 — PR draft → `block_reason` overlay (opt-in `draft_overlay`): mirror draft state onto the card, overlay-only (no column move)

**Date:** 2026-07-13
**Context:** A card whose PR is a **draft** should read as *blocked* on the board, but nothing surfaced it — the writeback only ever moved a card between columns (opened/merged/…), and the board's own "blocked" signal (`block_reason`, which also PINS a card against auto-move via DL-178) was human-only. Operators wanted a real-time draft↔`block_reason` mirror. Two shapes were on the table: move the card to a **Blocked column**, or **overlay** the `block_reason` field in place. The move-to-Blocked shape was **explicitly deferred** per operator direction — it drags a DL-163 no-regression/capture-restore problem in behind it (where does the card go, how does it come back, how does that interact with the terminal-stage guard). This round is the **overlay only**. Roundtable #18, card #4139.

**Decision:** add an opt-in per-mapping bool **`draft_overlay`** (default false) that, for a mapped repo, emits a new `kanban_block_reason` durable reaction mirroring the PR's draft state — **overlay ONLY, no stage/column move**. Three `pull_request` triggers, all driven by GitHub-controlled fields: **`converted_to_draft`** and **`opened`/`reopened` with `pull_request.draft === true`** → **SET**; **`ready_for_review`** → **CLEAR**. On an opened-as-draft PR the existing `opened` move STILL fires unchanged **in addition** — the overlay only appends the set target (distinct dispatch bucket `handler|debounceKey`, so the move and the overlay on the same card never coalesce). Correlation reuses the existing DL/`card#` try-in-order resolution (move ALL matching cards; no card token → no-op). `WritebackConfig::OUTCOMES` is **unchanged** — draft actions are not stage-mapped outcomes, so a pre-v0.20 malformed-config concern doesn't apply.

**Data-preservation (load-bearing — must never stomp a human's `block_reason`).** Both operations GET the card first (`KanbanBlockReasonHandler`): **SET = add-if-missing** — write the marker `"PR is in draft"` **only when `block_reason` is empty** (null/blank, matching PinGuard's trim semantics); any existing value (human reason, or our marker already there) is left → idempotent. **CLEAR = clear-if-ours** — null `block_reason` **only when it is exactly the marker**; a human reason is preserved. The marker string is the handler's single source (`KanbanBlockReasonHandler::MARKER`); the classifier emits only `action: set|clear`.

**Alternatives considered:** (a) **move to a Blocked column** — DEFERRED per operator direction (drags DL-163/capture-restore/parked-auto-unpark in; separate round). (b) **refactor the move path's FR-7 resolver into a shared primitive** both the move and overlay paths call — REJECTED for this change: the hard requirement is that existing move outcomes stay **byte-identical**, and the move path's resolver is entangled with move-only side effects (precedence/high-value-miss logging, `card#`-path stamp refs #3866). A separate `correlatedCardIds()` for the overlay (same resolution, no move-only logging — which would otherwise double-log an opened-as-draft event) keeps the move path untouched; a future unification can extract the skeleton once it can be done without disturbing the move side. (c) **an `alert_channel`-style notifier on the block_reason handler's permanent failures** — NOT adopted: the closest sibling opt-in handler (`KanbanDependabotCardHandler`) logs loudly without the notifier, and `WritebackAlertNotifier::notify` is outcome-shaped, not action-shaped; the handler fails loud via `Log::warning` on every permanent branch, matching the dependabot handler's posture.

**Load-bearing safety (verified in code + test):** (1) **byte-identical when off** — `draft_overlay` absent/false ⇒ `blockReasonTargets` is never called and `$overlayTargets` is `[]`, so every move-path return is `array_merge(move, [])` = move; the pure-draft actions (`converted_to_draft`/`ready_for_review`) return `[]` exactly as the old null-outcome early-return did (`test_converted_to_draft_is_noop_when_draft_overlay_off`, full existing move/dependabot suites green). (2) **dependabot path byte-identical** — its block is re-gated on `$outcome !== null`, reproducing the old "unreachable for a null-outcome action" behavior (it early-returned before). (3) **no PinGuard change** — the pin is a *consequence* of writing `block_reason`, read by the existing PinGuard; DL-178 untouched. (4) **security** — the handler enforces the same belongs-to-mapped-board guard and transient(5xx→retry)/permanent(4xx→log+no-op) split as the move handler; the card id rides as the target_id (numeric-string validated), repo/action are the only payload.

**Consequences:** `WritebackMapping`/`WritebackConfig` (parse `draft_overlay`, mirror `create_dependabot_cards`), `KanbanClient::setBlockReason` (thin `PATCH {task:{block_reason}}` verb, mirrors `moveCard`), `GitHubPrCardMoveClassifier` (draft-action → `kanban_block_reason` target(s), composing with the move path), new `KanbanBlockReasonHandler` (durable, idempotent, add-if-missing/clear-if-ours), `HandlerRegistry` (`kanban_block_reason` always-on, inert without config), `docs/writeback.md` + `docs/config-schema.md`. New tests: 10 classifier cases (set/clear/opened-as-draft-both/bundled/card#/off/no-token/unmapped) + a full `KanbanBlockReasonHandlerTest` (add-if-missing incl. whitespace boundary, clear-if-ours, guards, transient/permanent split, malformed payload). 672/672 phpunit, phpstan L7 0, pint clean. **No migration, no new `.env`, no change to what the receiver accepts/rejects.** Opt-in, default-off ⇒ every existing install byte-identical. Roundtable #18, card #4139.

## DL-194 — Auto-unpark a parked card on branch-cut (opt-in `unpark_from_stages`): reverse DL-178 for opt-in stages + a compensating override alert

**Date:** 2026-07-13
**Context:** The `started` writeback (DL-160, fires on a branch-create push) **refuses** to promote a *pinned* card (DL-178: non-empty `block_reason` OR a `no-automove` tag → log + `pinned_no_automove` alert + no move). So a card parked/gated and then resumed (a fresh branch cut for it) stays parked and the board drifts from reality at the exact moment a human took the clearest "work has begun" action. Roundtable #19 converged three-seat (both peer operators + kanban-solo ruled ADOPT, operator-APPROVED) on reversing this: **uniform move on a fresh branch-cut even from a parked stage; a marker gates an operator ALERT (not the move); a genuinely-held card must never be unparked silently.** The real enforcement gate lives at deploy/merge + a persistent tag — the column is not enforcement; the alert is the compensating "we overrode a human hold" notification. Scope is the BRIDGE `started`-path only; the toolkit `board-card-start` half + a Won't-Do-revival are separate builds. Card #4172.
